create DATABASE clinicMap
go
use ClinicMap
go


create table MemberStatus(
	memberStatusID varchar(3) primary key,
	status varchar(6) not null,
)
insert into MemberStatus(memberStatusID,status) values('MS0','未認證')
insert into MemberStatus(memberStatusID,status) values('MS1','有認證')

create table MemberGender(
	genderID varchar(3) primary key,
	memberGender varchar(4) not null,
)
insert into MemberGender(genderID,memberGender) values('MG1','男性')
insert into MemberGender(genderID,memberGender) values('MG2','女性')

create table Member(
	memberID int primary key identity(101,1),
	memberPhoto varbinary(max),
	memberAccount varchar(20) not null unique,
	memberName varchar(20) not null,
	memberPwd varchar(20) not null,
	memberBirth date not null,
    memberEmail varchar(50) not null,
	memberAddress varchar(50),
	memberHeight tinyint,
	memberWeight tinyint,
	memberPhone char(10) not null,
	memberIdNumber char(10) not null unique,
	memberGender varchar(3) FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES MemberGender(genderID),
	memberStatus varchar(3) FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES MemberStatus(memberStatusID),
	memberVerifiedCode nvarchar(32),
	memberRegisterDeadline bigint
)
insert Member (memberAccount,memberName,memberEmail ,memberPwd,memberBirth,memberAddress,memberHeight,memberWeight,memberPhone,memberIdNumber,memberGender,memberStatus) 
            values('user1223','jay','a29536693@gmail.com','abc123','1990/11/15','25.0384077,121.541256',172,85,'0935336262','A123456729','MG1','MS1')

create table ClinicClass(
	clinicClassID int primary key identity(1001,1),
	clinicClass varchar(20) not null,
)

create table ClinicType(
	clinicTypeID int primary key identity(2001,1),
	clinicType varchar(20) not null,
)

create table ClinicStatus(
	clinicStatusID varchar(3) primary key,
	clinicStatus varchar(6) not null,
)
insert into ClinicStatus(clinicStatusID,clinicStatus) values('CS0','未認證')
insert into ClinicStatus(clinicStatusID,clinicStatus) values('CS1','有認證')

create table ClinicTime(
	ClinicTimeID varchar(4) primary key,
	ClinicTime varchar(10) not null,
)

create table Clinic(
	clinicID int primary key identity(1000,1),
	clinicName nvarchar(50) not null,
	clinicAccount varchar(50) not null unique,
	clinicPwd varchar(50) not null,
	clinicAddress nvarchar(150) not null,
	clinicDescription nvarchar(1000),
	clinicPhoto varbinary(max),
	clinicPhone varchar(50),
	clinicEmail nvarchar(50),
	clinicClass nvarchar(50),
	clinicType nvarchar(200),
	clinicTime varchar(50),
    cliniclat nvarchar(100),
    cliniclng nvarchar(100),
	clinicStatus varchar(3) FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES ClinicStatus(clinicStatusID),
)
create table ClinicOpenStatus(
clinicID int primary key FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES Clinic(clinicID),
clinicOpenStatus bit,
clinicCurrentNumber int,
)
create table NewsLetter(
	newsLetterClinic varchar(200) not null,
	newsLetterMember varchar(200) not null,
	newsLetterOrder varchar(200) not null,
	newsLetterOrderMiss varchar(200) not null,
)

create table AppointmentStatus(
	appointmentStatusID varchar(3) primary key,
	appointmentStatus varchar(10),
)
insert into AppointmentStatus(appointmentStatusID,appointmentStatus) values('OS1','預約')
insert into AppointmentStatus(appointmentStatusID,appointmentStatus) values('OS2','診療中')
insert into AppointmentStatus(appointmentStatusID,appointmentStatus) values('OS3','已看診')
insert into AppointmentStatus(appointmentStatusID,appointmentStatus) values('OS4','已過號')

create table AppointmentType(
	appointmentTypeID varchar(3) primary key,
	appointmentType varchar(4),
)
insert into AppointmentType(appointmentTypeID,appointmentType) values('OT1','複診')
insert into AppointmentType(appointmentTypeID,appointmentType) values('OT2','初診')

create table Appointment(
	appointmentID varchar(50) primary key,
	memberID int FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES Member(memberID),
	clinicID int FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES Clinic(clinicID),
	appointmentType varchar(3) FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES AppointmentType(appointmentTypeID),
	appointmentSickDescription nvarchar(200),
	appointmentTime datetime,
	appointmentNumber int,
	appointmentStatus varchar(3) FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES AppointmentStatus(appointmentStatusID),
)
select * from Appointment where clinicID='23188' and appointmentTime > '20200411' and AppointmentStatus='os1'
select * from clinic where clinicAccount ='3501011500'

create table Rearend(
	rearendID varchar(20) primary key,
	rearendPwd varchar(20) not null,
)

create table Sponsor(
	sponsorID varchar(20) primary key,
	clinicID int FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES Clinic(clinicID),
	sponsorTime smalldatetime,
)

create table Evaluation_Message(
	messageID int primary key,
	clinicID int FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES Clinic(clinicID),
	appointmentID varchar(50) FOREIGN KEY REFERENCES Appointment(appointmentID),
	Evaluation tinyint not null,
	Message nvarchar(50),
	evaluationTime date not null,
)
Create Table Sponsor(
	sponsorID int Primary Key Identity(1,1) not null,
	clinicAccount varchar(50) not null,
	tradeID varchar(50) not null,
	sponsorTime varchar(50) not null

)

Go
insert into ClinicStatus(clinicStatusID,clinicStatus) values('CS0','未認證')
insert into ClinicStatus(clinicStatusID,clinicStatus) values('CS1','有認證')
insert into ClinicStatus(clinicStatusID,clinicStatus) values('CS2','有認證且有贊助')
Go
Create Table SysManagement(
	ID int Primary Key Identity (1,1) not null ,
	sysAccount varchar (50) not null unique,
	sysPwd varchar(30) not null
)
